Support

Product support included

What's Product Support?

In the event your product doesn't work as expected or you need help using it, Amazon offers free product support options such as live phone/chat with an Amazon associate, manufacturer contact information, step-by-step troubleshooting guides, and help videos.
By solving product issues, we help the planet by extending the life of products. Availability of support options differ by product and country.  [Learn more](/ps/product-support?ref_=dp_pls_support&ref_=dp_ret_policy)

Your transaction is secure

We work hard to protect your security and privacy. Our payment security system encrypts your information during transmission. We don’t share your credit card details with third-party sellers, and we don’t sell your information to others.  [Learn more](/gp/help/customer/display.html?nodeId=201909010)

## Sustainability features

Energy efficiency

Conserves energy compared to similar products.

## ECOLOGO

---

ECOLOGO certified products are made with materials that reduce environmental impact at one or more stages of their life cycle, from raw materials to end of life. An ECOLOGO certification indicates that a product has met environmental performance standards, which include criteria in some or all of the following categories: materials, energy, manufacturing and operations, health and environment, product performance and use, and product stewardship and innovation. Products are evaluated on the applicable criteria through testing and auditing.

[Learn more about this certification](https://www.ul.com/resources/ecologo-certification-program)

Safer chemicals

Made with chemicals safer for human health and the environment.

As certified by

ECOLOGO

How trade-in works

How trade-in works

![Upgrade and save](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_delivery.png)

1. Upgrade and save

Accept your estimated trade-in value, buy your new device at the current price, and receive your delivery.

![Prepare device](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_tell_us.png)

2. Prepare device

Sign out of all accounts linked to your old device, and factory reset it to erase your personal information.

![Ship within 30 days](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_send.png)

3. Ship within 30 days

Print your shipping label, [package your old device](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=G2Q9VNXJ29E7AK89), and drop it off at any UPS location within 30 days of receiving your new device.

![Get your rebate](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/2_how_rebate.png)

4. Get your rebate

After we receive your trade-in device, we'll verify it within 10 business days. Once verified, you'll receive your [trade-in value](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=GNESDAAB2JL84N3A) as an Amazon.com Gift Card to your Amazon account for immediate use.

# About this item

* Google Pixel 10 is the everyday phone unlike anything else; it has Google Tensor G5, Pixel’s most powerful chip, an incredible camera, and advanced AI - Gemini built in[1]
* Unlocked Android phone gives you the flexibility to change carriers and choose your own data plan[2]; it works - Google Fi, Verizon, T-Mobile, AT&T, and other major carriers
* The upgraded triple rear camera system has a new 5x telephoto lens - up to 20x Super Res Zoom for stunning detail from far away; Night Sight takes crisp, clear photos in low-light settings; and Camera Coach helps you snap your best pics[3]
* Pixel 10 is designed - scratch-resistant Corning Gorilla Glass Victus 2 and has an IP68 rating for water and dust protection[21]; plus, the Actua display - 3,000-nit peak brightness is easy on the eyes, even in direct sunlight[4]
* Instead of typing, use Gemini Live to have a natural, free-flowing conversation; point your camera at what you're curious about – like a sea creature at the aquarium – or chat - Gemini to brainstorm ideas or get things done across apps[5]

   ## ECOLOGO

   ---

   ECOLOGO certified products are made with materials that reduce environmental impact at one or more stages of their life cycle, from raw materials to end of life. An ECOLOGO certification indicates that a product has met environmental performance standards, which include criteria in some or all of the following categories: materials, energy, manufacturing and operations, health and environment, product performance and use, and product stewardship and innovation. Products are evaluated on the applicable criteria through testing and auditing.

   ## ECOLOGO

   ---

   ECOLOGO certified products are made with materials that reduce environmental impact at one or more stages of their life cycle, from raw materials to end of life. An ECOLOGO certification indicates that a product has met environmental performance standards, which include criteria in some or all of the following categories: materials, energy, manufacturing and operations, health and environment, product performance and use, and product stewardship and innovation. Products are evaluated on the applicable criteria through testing and auditing.

## Product Description

Escape the ordinary - Google Pixel 10. It has Pixel’s most powerful chip, an incredible camera, and Gemini built in to supercharge your productivity and creativity.[1] The Google One Premium 2TB plan, Fitbit Premium, and YouTube Premium trial offers are available to eligible users of each service with the purchase and activation of Pixel 10. Offers expire at 11:59 pm PT on October 31, 2026. Valid form of payment required at sign-up, but you will not be charged the $9.99/mo for Google One, $9.99/mo for Fitbit Premium or $13.99/mo for YouTube Premium until the respective trial period expires and the subscriptions auto-renew. Cancel anytime. Return of purchased device may result in cancellation of all subscriptions. Fitbit Premium content and features may change, are not available in all countries, and may be in English only. See gstore for more information

How customer reviews and ratings work

Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say

Customers find this phone to be a solid device with impressive camera capabilities, particularly noting its high-resolution images. The phone is straightforward to set up, especially with eSIM configuration, and customers appreciate its features, battery life, and value for money. They like its appearance, with one customer noting it maintains its best appearance without manual editing. The functionality receives mixed reviews, with some saying it performs as expected while others report issues with certain apps.

It works good with straight talk wireless once you get everything transferred correctly. The face recognition and fingerprint features work great on this one. They have done really good at improving the fingerprint sensing abilities. The battery lasts about 24 hours depending on how much I use it. I have a lot of apps that run in the background for alarms and cameras. This is a great phone and a great price!

  ##### [*5.0 out of 5 stars* Excellent quality](/gp/customer-reviews/R1YYC3JLA9RAFS/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

  Reviewed in the United States on August 29, 2025

  Color: IndigoSize: 256GBStyle: Pixel 10 (Phone Only)[Verified Purchase](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

  The good stuff:
  - great looks and feels great in your hand (excellent quality feel)
  - excellent screen
  - always fresh and in active development directly from original Android source
  - best camera on the market

  Neutral:
  - speed is very slowly improving (if at all)
  - not many extras in the packaging (e.g., no wall power adapter)
  - I like bit smaller phones in general (Pixel 5 was an ideal size for me)
  - AI emphasized too much (and not used at all by me). Hopefully AI is not using any resources while supposedly idle.

  Don't like:
  - Slow or troublesome START and RESTART, frequently having to keep pressing the START button for 20 secs or so. I had experience with Pixel 4, 5, 6a, and 7 and never had that experience (UPDATE: This seems to be no problem any longer after an update)
  - No instructions of any kind in the box, although it's rather intuitive once you start the new phone
  - No physical SIM card slot for the US customers (only, so-called, eSIM from your service provider). A bit unnerving since my phones were usually successfully fixed or transferred to a different service in the past by changing of SIM cards -- it will take a decade or so of trouble-free experience to forget about that small card
  - For some reason, turning off Bluetooth (for us who don't use it very often) requires a post-doctoral degree (Bluetooth turns itself ON automatically after some time)

  Note: I use Google Fi service.

  Read more

  ##### [*4.0 out of 5 stars* Good, tough coming from iPhone](/gp/customer-reviews/R2TJW81DDPQAXC/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

  Reviewed in the United States on January 25, 2026

  Color: FrostSize: 256GBStyle: Pixel 10 (Phone Only)[Verified Purchase](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

  I switched from an iPhone 15 nearly 3 months ago. It was pretty easy to setup this phone on my own and this is a nice device.

  There are some things about the android that are better than the iPhone, but there are some drawbacks too.

  The good:

  I like the notifications a lot better.
  I like how customizable everything is.
  I think it connects to Bluetooth devices faster.
  The phone doesn't come with a bunch of bloatware.
  The camera is amazing.
  The battery life is better than iPhone was when it was new.

  The trade offs

  1. The face unlock doesn't work unless it's bright in the room. Very frustrating if you're used to Face ID.

  2. The user experience isn't consistent. Copy paste, undo, etc are in different places depending on what you're doing. Feels like android was built by many different programmers and cobbled together.

  3. Several apps don't work correctly or look schlocky compared to how they did on my iPhone.

  4. Many tasks take more effort - here are just a couple examples

  Sending pics within the messages app - you can do this, but you can't zoom, crop, edit or write on the photo before sending within messages. You need to open up camera, take the pic, do the edits, save, then open messages and send the photo. Poorly thought out workflow.

  Silencing the ringer - iPhone you flip a tiny switch without even glancing at the phone or taking it out of your pocket. Android requires you to press the volume button then press two buttons on the screen. It's not the end of the world, but very inconvenient when having a face to face conversation with someone and want to silence my phone.

  5. I miss iMessage because editing texts after sending them was really handy. Big step backwards

  6. No shake to undo. Accidentally delete a photo or email, change the wrong setting? Shake to undo. With Android, go to deleted photos or emails, locate the photo and undelete.

  My hope is that I end up learning more and finding out that everything above is incorrect and I just didn't have enough experience with the phone yet.

  If I had to guess based on my experience so far, I will keep this phone for a few years, but when it's time to upgrade, I'll probably go back to an iPhone.

  But to be clear, I don't think it's the Pixel's fault, it's Android.

  Read more

  Ángel Rodríguez

  *5.0 out of 5 stars*

  ##### Buen equipo, logística rara

  Reviewed in Mexico on February 3, 2026

  Un gran equipo, el proceso de envio fue medio gris porque tardo en notificar su llegada, no habia forma de contactar a nadie y aunque decía que viene de EUA, la etiqueta de envio de la paquetería fue programada en Cancún, fuera de ello el equipo no ha dado problemas, viene como se esperaba, nuevo, funciona bien, obviamente ya no trae cubo de carga, solo el simple y llano cable Tipo C. Tiene tamaño cómodo para usarse con una sola mano, aunque, si vienes de un movil grande te resultara pequeño. Se desempeña bien, y si no te interesa el rendimiento en juegos que es lo que generalmente se encuentra como lo negativo, te ira perfecto, no hay que bajar mas y mas y mas aplicaciones, mientras tengas una cuenta google todo se armoniza. Por cierto el “blanco” es mas bien un lila claro, para tenerlo en mente.

Support

Product support included

What's Product Support?

In the event your product doesn't work as expected or you need help using it, Amazon offers free product support options such as live phone/chat with an Amazon associate, manufacturer contact information, step-by-step troubleshooting guides, and help videos.
By solving product issues, we help the planet by extending the life of products. Availability of support options differ by product and country.  [Learn more](/ps/product-support?ref_=dp_pls_support&ref_=dp_ret_policy)

Packaging

Ships in product packaging

![black leaf](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/siocLanding/icon-sustainability-20-black-2x.png)  Ships in product packaging

This item has been tested to certify it can ship safely in its original box or bag to avoid unnecessary packaging. Since 2015, we have reduced the weight of outbound packaging per shipment by 41% on average, that’s over 2 million tons of packaging material.

*If you still require Amazon packaging for this item, choose "Ship in Amazon packaging" at checkout.*   [Learn more](/sipp_home)

How trade-in works

How trade-in works

![Upgrade and save](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_delivery.png)

1. Upgrade and save

Accept your estimated trade-in value, buy your new device at the current price, and receive your delivery.

![Prepare device](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_tell_us.png)

2. Prepare device

Sign out of all accounts linked to your old device, and factory reset it to erase your personal information.

![Ship within 30 days](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_send.png)

3. Ship within 30 days

Print your shipping label, [package your old device](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=G2Q9VNXJ29E7AK89), and drop it off at any UPS location within 30 days of receiving your new device.

![Get your rebate](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/2_how_rebate.png)

4. Get your rebate

After we receive your trade-in device, we'll verify it within 10 business days. Once verified, you'll receive your [trade-in value](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=GNESDAAB2JL84N3A) as an Amazon.com Gift Card to your Amazon account for immediate use.

## What is Amazon Renewed?

Amazon Renewed is your trusted destination for products that are inspected, tested, and refurbished as necessary to be fully functional.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11X1grO0K6L.png)

#### Quality you can afford

Amazon Renewed products offer an affordable option so you can save on the brands you love.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11m5NyTwLVL.png)

#### Products you can trust

All products have been professionally inspected, tested, cleaned, and refurbished as necessary by Amazon-qualified suppliers. Products are not certified by Apple.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11MpO5lMksL.png)

#### Purchases with an impact

Your Amazon Renewed purchase extends the lifetime of this product and reduces electronic waste.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/118nlf+F3RL.png)

#### Trusted coverage

Your purchase is eligible for Amazon Renewed coverage in conjunction with Amazon's Return Policy and the A-to-z Guarantee.

#### What should I expect to receive with my Amazon Renewed purchase?

All Amazon Renewed purchases will come with accessories equivalent to those that shipped in the box when new. These items may not be original but will be compatible and fully functional. Amazon Renewed products will be packaged in either original packaging or in a new and clean cardboard box.

#### Model Year

2023

#### In what condition can I expect my Amazon Renewed product to be?

Product will be restored to its original factory settings and will be in one of the following cosmetic conditions Premium, Excellent, Good or Acceptable. [Learn more](/gp/help/customer/display.html?nodeId=202089470)

Shop for smartphones, computers, laptops, tablets, home and kitchen appliances, game consoles, office products, and more. [Visit Amazon Renewed](/renewed)

How customer reviews and ratings work

Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say

Customers find the iPhone to be in perfect condition, like new, with a 100% battery life and good value for money. They appreciate its appearance, noting it looks like new with brand new screen and case, and one customer mentions the speakers work great. The phone's functionality receives mixed feedback, with some reporting it works like new while others say it doesn't work properly. Similarly, the unlock status is mixed, with some customers confirming it's unlocked while others report it being locked. The scratch resistance also gets mixed reviews, with some customers reporting no scratches while others mention scratches on the screen.

##### Definitely worth upgrading (Premium Unlocked)

So far so good. Transferring esim is easier than I thought. I got the premium unlocked and the maximum capacity is not bad. Camera quality is amazing compared to my 4 years old phone. It feels nice and new. No scratches, dent, or discoloration. It looks durable. And the green color is amazing in person. Definitely worth it if you're under budget. I would highly get the premium one.

Support

Product support included

What's Product Support?

In the event your product doesn't work as expected or you need help using it, Amazon offers free product support options such as live phone/chat with an Amazon associate, manufacturer contact information, step-by-step troubleshooting guides, and help videos.
By solving product issues, we help the planet by extending the life of products. Availability of support options differ by product and country.  [Learn more](/ps/product-support?ref_=dp_pls_support&ref_=dp_ret_policy)

Get your estimated trade-in value

How trade-in works

How trade-in works

![Upgrade and save](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_delivery.png)

1. Upgrade and save

Accept your estimated trade-in value, buy your new device at the current price, and receive your delivery.

![Prepare device](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_tell_us.png)

2. Prepare device

Sign out of all accounts linked to your old device, and factory reset it to erase your personal information.

![Ship within 30 days](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_send.png)

3. Ship within 30 days

Print your shipping label, [package your old device](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=G2Q9VNXJ29E7AK89), and drop it off at any UPS location within 30 days of receiving your new device.

![Get your rebate](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/2_how_rebate.png)

4. Get your rebate

After we receive your trade-in device, we'll verify it within 10 business days. Once verified, you'll receive your [trade-in value](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=GNESDAAB2JL84N3A) as an Amazon.com Gift Card to your Amazon account for immediate use.

Sorry, we're unable to process your trade-in, try again later

## What is Amazon Renewed?

Amazon Renewed is your trusted destination for products that are inspected, tested, and refurbished as necessary to be fully functional.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11X1grO0K6L.png)

#### Quality you can afford

Amazon Renewed products offer an affordable option so you can save on the brands you love.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11m5NyTwLVL.png)

#### Products you can trust

All products have been professionally inspected, tested, cleaned, and refurbished as necessary by Amazon-qualified suppliers. Products are not certified by Apple.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11MpO5lMksL.png)

#### Purchases with an impact

Your Amazon Renewed purchase extends the lifetime of this product and reduces electronic waste.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/118nlf+F3RL.png)

#### Trusted coverage

Your purchase is eligible for Amazon Renewed coverage in conjunction with Amazon's Return Policy and the A-to-z Guarantee.

#### What should I expect to receive with my Amazon Renewed purchase?

All Amazon Renewed purchases will come with accessories equivalent to those that shipped in the box when new. These items may not be original but will be compatible and fully functional. Amazon Renewed products will be packaged in either original packaging or in a new and clean cardboard box.

#### Model Year

2021

#### In what condition can I expect my Amazon Renewed product to be?

Product will be restored to its original factory settings and will be in one of the following cosmetic conditions Premium, Excellent, Good or Acceptable. [Learn more](/gp/help/customer/display.html?nodeId=202089470)

Shop for smartphones, computers, laptops, tablets, home and kitchen appliances, game consoles, office products, and more. [Visit Amazon Renewed](/renewed)

## Product Description

The iPhone 13 features a 6.1-inch (155 mm) display with Super Retina XDR OLED technology at a resolution of 2532×1170 pixels and a pixel density of about 460 PPI with a refresh rate of 60 Hz and Dolby Vision HDR. Additional features include a dual-camera system, consisting of a 12MP F1.6 wide-angle and another 12MP F2.4 ultra-wide camera with True Tone flash and lens correction. Both rear cameras have larger sensors with improved light sensitivity and Dolby Vision HDR video recording, but only digital zoom and no optical zoom. The front-facing ultra-wide camera is a 12MP F2.2 one. The iPhone 13 video recording supports 4K videos at 60fps as well as 1080p video at up to 240fps. The iPhone 13 model is available in six colors: Midnight, Starlight, Product Red, Blue, Pink, and Green.

How customer reviews and ratings work

Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say

Customers find the iPhone 13 like new, with excellent condition and brand new appearance. The phone receives positive feedback for its quality, value for money, and functionality, with many saying it works like new. However, battery life and functionality show mixed results - while some report 100% battery health, others experience poor battery life, and some units stop working. The phone's condition is generally good, with no scratches or damage reported.

It does come in just a cardboard box and not an iPhone box, but I had an old one laying around to put it in. So that my son could feel like he was getting a brand new phone.   ##### *5.0 out of 5 stars* Nice iphone

  Reviewed in Canada on November 26, 2024

  Size: 128GBColor: (PRODUCT)REDService provider: UnlockedProduct grade: Renewed Premium[Verified Purchase](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

  While I know it came out three years ago. It is much newer than my phone that came out 7 years ago.

  I had never seen the “premium” condition for an iPhone.

  When I received I can not find one scratch, dent or mark on the phone. The battery was 93%.

  While I would have liked a better percentage. I received exactly what they claimed in the description.

  No complaints at all.

  It has only been a couple days since buying. I am really happy with this purchase.

  While there was an “excellent”condition iPhone, same as this one. Which was also cheaper. I do not regret getting this “premium,” phone.

  It has a one year warranty with Amazon. Which you don’t get on anything in less condition.

  With it being shipped and sold by Amazon I felt that also was in my favour.

  As of now I would buy and recommend buying a refurbished phone from Amazon. Whichever seller is up to you. AA has always worked for me.

  HIGHLY RECOMMEND!!
